owbcpcsn_debug_decisions = {
	nr_enc_puppet_recolor = {
		cost = 0
		fire_only_once = no
		available = {
			NEW = {
				has_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_cosmetic_tag
			}
			is_subject_of = NEW
			is_ai = yes
			has_global_flag = owbcpcsn_switch_on_names_flag 
		}
		visible = { 
			is_ai = yes
			is_subject = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
		  factor = 1000
		}
		complete_effect = {
			##Merged Puppets
			##NCR
			#Whole Bear
			if = { limit = { OR = { TAG = NCR TAG = BON TAG = BAR TAG = DAY } has_full_control_of_state = 135 has_full_control_of_state = 253 has_full_control_of_state = 350  has_full_control_of_state = 63 OVERLORD = { has_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_cosmetic_tag }} set_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_Whole_Bear set_country_flag = color_changed }
			#North Bear
			if = { limit = { OR = { TAG = NCR TAG = BON TAG = BAR } OR = { AND = { has_full_control_of_state = 135 has_full_control_of_state = 253 has_full_control_of_state = 350 NOT = { has_full_control_of_state = 63 }} AND = { has_full_control_of_state = 135 has_full_control_of_state = 253 NOT = { has_full_control_of_state = 63 has_full_control_of_state = 350 }}} OVERLORD = { has_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_cosmetic_tag }} set_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_North_Bear set_country_flag = color_changed }
			#South Bear
			if = { limit = { OR = { TAG = NCR TAG = BON TAG = DAY } OR = { AND = { has_full_control_of_state = 253 has_full_control_of_state = 350 has_full_control_of_state = 63  NOT = { has_full_control_of_state = 135 }} AND = { has_full_control_of_state = 350 has_full_control_of_state = 63 NOT = { has_full_control_of_state = 135 has_full_control_of_state = 253 }}} OVERLORD = { has_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_cosmetic_tag }} set_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_South_Bear set_country_flag = color_changed }
			#Central Bear
			if = { limit = { OR = { TAG = NCR TAG = BON } has_full_control_of_state = 253 has_full_control_of_state = 350 NOT = { has_full_control_of_state = 135 has_full_control_of_state = 63 }} OVERLORD = { has_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_cosmetic_tag } set_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_Centr_Bear set_country_flag = color_changed }

			#Checks
			if = { limit = { OR = { TAG = NCR TAG = BAR } has_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_North_Bear BON = { NOT = { has_full_control_of_state = 63 }}} BON = { set_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_Centr_Bear set_country_flag = color_changed }}

			if = { limit = { OR = { TAG = NCR TAG = BAR } has_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_North_Bear BON = { has_full_control_of_state = 350 has_full_control_of_state = 63 }} BON = { set_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_South_Bear set_country_flag = color_changed }}

			if = { limit = { OR = { TAG = NCR TAG = BAR } has_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_North_Bear DAY = { has_full_control_of_state = 350 has_full_control_of_state = 63 }} DAY = { set_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_South_Bear set_country_flag = color_changed }}

			if = { limit = { OR = { TAG = BON TAG = DAY } has_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_South_Bear NCR = { NOT = { has_full_control_of_state = 135 }}} NCR = { set_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_Centr_Bear set_country_flag = color_changed }}

			if = { limit = { OR = { TAG = BON TAG = DAY } has_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_South_Bear NCR = { NOT = { has_full_control_of_state = 135 }}} NCR = { set_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_Centr_Bear set_country_flag = color_changed }}

			##Baja BLP+BVC
			if = { limit = { OR = { TAG = BLP TAG = BVC TAG = BJS } has_full_control_of_state = 41 has_full_control_of_state = 97 OVERLORD = { has_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_cosmetic_tag }} set_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_Whole_Baja set_country_flag = color_changed }

			##Tllaloc TLA
			if = { limit = { has_full_control_of_state = 769 OVERLORD = { has_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_cosmetic_tag }} set_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_TLA set_country_flag = color_changed }

			##Idaho
			if = { limit = { OR = { TAG = HEA TAG = HGH } has_full_control_of_state = 116 has_full_control_of_state = 140 OVERLORD = { has_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_cosmetic_tag }} set_cosmetic_tag = cpcsn_ENC_Whole_Idah set_country_flag = color_changed }
		}
	}

		cost = 0

		cost = 0
		fire_only_once = no
		available = {
			has_global_flag = owbcpcsn_switch_off_names_flag
			is_subject = yes
			is_ai = yes
		}
		visible = { 
			is_ai = yes
			is_subject = yes
		}
		ai_will_do = {
		  factor = 1000
		}
		complete_effect = {
			if = { limit = { is_subject_of = NCR } drop_cosmetic_tag = yes set_country_flag = name_removed clr_country_flag = colored_puppet clr_country_flag = color_changed }
			if = { limit = { is_subject_of = CES } drop_cosmetic_tag = yes set_country_flag = name_removed clr_country_flag = colored_puppet }
			if = { limit = { is_subject_of = BOS } drop_cosmetic_tag = yes set_country_flag = name_removed clr_country_flag = colored_puppet }
			if = { limit = { OVERLORD = { tag = NEW has_country_flag = enclave_nation }} drop_cosmetic_tag = yes set_country_flag = name_removed clr_country_flag = colored_puppet }
		}
